         }
      });
   }
   var sortObjects = function() {
      objects.sort(function(a, b){
         var c=new Date(a.date);
         var d=new Date(b.date);
         return c-d;
      });
   }   
   
   var printObjects = function(){

         var ul = document.createElement('ul');
      	ul.setAttribute("class","evenemangslist");
         div.appendChild(ul);

         var a;
         var element; 
         jq.each(objects,function(i,item) {

    			eventAddress = eventAddress.replace(/\s/ig,"-");                        
            eventAddress = encodeURIComponent( eventAddress )

            eventAddress = eventAddress
            .replace(/%2C/g, '')
            .replace(/%B7/g, '')
            .replace(/%26-/g, '')
            ;
            
            /*
            eventAddress = eventAddress
            .replace(/%26/g, '')

            .replace(/%D6/g, 'o')  				
            .replace(/%26acirc%3B/g, 'a') 
            .replace(/%C2/g, 'a')
            .replace(/%E2/g, 'a')
            .replace(/%26eacute%3B/g, 'e') 
            .replace(/%E9/g, 'e')
            .replace(/%26Eacute%3B/g, 'E')
            .replace(/%C9/g, 'e')

            */
				
            
            
            
            if(i < count) {
               element = document.createElement('li');
               element.setAttribute("data",i.toString());
               element.setAttribute("class","evenemangsitem");
               li = element;
               ul.appendChild(element);
               


               if(datumFormat !== ""){
                                                    
                  element = document.createElement('div');
                  element.setAttribute("class","evenemangxdatum");
                  var strDate = moment(item.date).format(datumFormat);
                  strDate = strDate.replace("00.00","");
                  if(item.endDate > item.date){
                     strDate += " - " + moment(item.endDate).format("YYYY-MM-DD");
                     //strDate += " - " +endDate.replace("00.00","");
                  }
                  
                  element.innerHTML = strDate;
                  li.appendChild(element);
                  
                  
               }

               element = document.createElement('div');
               element.setAttribute("class","itemcontainer");
               div = element;
               li.appendChild(element);
               */

               element.setAttribute("class","chevron fa-chevron-right");
               //div.appendChild(element);
               li.appendChild(element);
               
                            
                             
               element = document.createElement('a');
               element.setAttribute("href",produktURL + eventAddress + "-" + item.id);
               element.innerHTML = item.title;
               element.setAttribute("class","evenemang normal");
               //div.appendChild(element);
               li.appendChild(element);
			   
			   
               
               if(visaText === 'Ja'){
                  element = document.createElement('a');
                  element.setAttribute("href",produktURL + eventAddress + "-" + item.id);
                  element.setAttribute("class","text BODY");
                  if(antalTecken != 0 && item.text.length > antalTecken){
                     element.innerHTML = item.text.substring(0,antalTecken);
                  }
                  else {
                     element.innerHTML = item.text;
                  }
                  li.appendChild(element);
               }
               
               if(visaBild == 'Ja' && item.pic != false)
               {
                 element = document.createElement('img');
                 element.src = item.pic[0].url_medium;
                 li.appendChild(element);
               }

            }
            else {
               return false;
            }
         });

      printObjects();
